<div id="review_271567900" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/271567900" />
    <a title="Doreen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6905976-doreen"><img alt="Doreen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1327852895p2/6905976.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/271567900?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Doreen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Doreen" href="/user/show/6905976-doreen">Doreen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer271567900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6189388749910183387">To start off. I do not understand the logic in leaving to save people. Has no one but myself heard of strength in numbers? I understand that this is fiction but what does it really say about how we as humans think strategically. I mean what good can one possibly do by leaving? You end up worrying the people you left and they end up being so distracted that they end up captured or worse DEAD. If ever I were in a situation where every supernatural being out there either wanted me as their "pet" or</span>
  <span id="freeText6189388749910183387" style="display:none">To start off. I do not understand the logic in leaving to save people. Has no one but myself heard of strength in numbers? I understand that this is fiction but what does it really say about how we as humans think strategically. I mean what good can one possibly do by leaving? You end up worrying the people you left and they end up being so distracted that they end up captured or worse DEAD. If ever I were in a situation where every supernatural being out there either wanted me as their "pet" or wanted me dead? I'd like to think that I'll have a decent support system instead of running off to save them..........NO. It's noble, I'd think long and hard about it but I'd feel like I can save them by keeping myself alive. This beggining however doesn't tell you why I gave this book five stars considering its a negative. The main reason that this gets a five star is because I love how its written! OMG is just beautiful. Then the characters. Evie's angel friends aside *please make Zee more enjoyable I feel like he could be funnier!* RUSSELL! He gets better and better and better! I feel like he is MY soulmate. I cannot love any character more. Then we have Finn. Accent aside *I barely understand the guy* he is just lovely in that medival kind of way. Last but certainly not the least. Preben! His name is a little on the weird side like something you would call a sleep enducing drug BUT he touched my heart Preben did. He reminded me of that character in twilight that was part of the Volturi that no one ever notices because they are too preoccupied with Edward. I would like more of Preben because he amuses me just like that Volturi guy that I loved but never got to see. <br />I'd like to pick a bone with the whole sex on the beach thing. Its a decent cocktail but not a decent act. You get sand in places sand definetly isn't meant to be. No matter how lovely it sounds in books, there should be a warning caption not to try it at home or on vacation or whatever. I wish authors wouldn't write scenes like that in their books. Its like false advertisment. What ever happened to you know KING SIZE BEDS WITH ROSES! Or some other cheesy stuff. Call me old fashioned but that sounds more appealing. <br />I cannot wait for the next book that hopefully consists of more of EVIE'S wit that I've come to enjoy so much. More of Russell and Preben too!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6189388749910183387" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText3398731742701527131" style="display:none">*Reread September 2015*<br /><br />I'm knocking my rating down one star. <div id="review_257704832" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/257704832" />
    <a title="Suike" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5718370-suike"><img alt="Suike" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/257704832?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suike" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suike" href="/user/show/5718370-suike">Suike</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer257704832" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13391265172698866381">I am really enjoying this series. I was completely surprised when I read the first book of the series and the second did not disappoint. <br/><br/>The romance between Evie and Reed was just as wonderful and the author does a great job in making me emotionally attached to them. Although there were times where Evie was a bit frustrating as her thoughts would sometimes stray to Russell. I hope that in the third book, Evie is completely over the whole soul mate issue and Russell finds a new love interest.<br/><br/>A ne</span>
  <span id="freeText13391265172698866381" style="display:none">I am really enjoying this series. I was completely surprised when I read the first book of the series and the second did not disappoint. <br /><br />The romance between Evie and Reed was just as wonderful and the author does a great job in making me emotionally attached to them. Although there were times where Evie was a bit frustrating as her thoughts would sometimes stray to Russell. I hope that in the third book, Evie is completely over the whole soul mate issue and Russell finds a new love interest.<br /><br />A new villain is introduced in this book which I find to be exciting. In most series, the villains stay constant so its refreshing to see that it won't be dragging on through the series. <br /><br />I did not end up giving it five stars though as there were certain parts that seem to drag a bit but I still manage to read it in one day. I differently recommend anyone whose interested in a new YA Paranormal series give this one a try.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13391265172698866381" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vUm1LNsqsxcEQ9hYdrtJwQS+AOuYiFpZQthI4m70m+Tkwba3Nj2pNgIq7ByQuF4jQBKEvX1jDQu7nzs7VY90OQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  }

  <span id="freeText10077442989173408378" style="display:none">Author of the Secondborn Series:<br />Secondborn (Book 1)<br />Traitor Born (Book 2)<br />Rebel Born (Book 3) <br /><br />Author of the Premonition Series:<br />Inescapable (Book 1) <br />Intuition (Book 2)<br />Indebted (Book 3)<br />Incendiary (Book 4) <br />Iniquity (Book 5) <br /><br />Author of the Kricket Series:<br />Under Different Stars (Book 1) <br />Sea of Stars (Book 2)<br />Darken the Stars (Book 3)<br /><br />The Divided - A Science Fiction Romance short story, which is included in the Take Me To Your Reader: An Otherworld Anthology. <br /><br />Amy A. Bartol is the USA Today and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of The Secondborn Series, The Premonition Series, The Kricket Series, and a short story entitled “The Divided.” She has won numerous awards for her writing and been nominated for several more. She's a graduate of Hillsdale College, which inspired the setting of her Premonition Series. Amy lives in Michigan with her husband and two sons, but she travels often, sparking her imagination to create more worlds like the ones with hidden angels, doorways to alien landscapes, and fantastical futuristic societies and technologies. To learn more, visit Amy's website at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.amyabartol.com">https://www.amyabartol.com</a></span>

            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Sometimes, I think I have made you up just to torture myself- and there are other times that I know you must be real because I couldn't have dreamed such perfection.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;

            <span class="readable">&ldquo;I ask God to bind my life to your life so that my mind will be one with your mind," I repeat the words Phaedrus says while I gaze at Reed and hold his hand. "My heart may be one with your heart," I recite it with a small smile on my face, "and my body may be one with your body," I blush a little when I say this part, seeing desire register in Reed's eyes. "From this moment through eternity, so let it be.&rdquo;</span>
